Protocol Title:  A Multicenter, Open-label Study to Assess the Long-term Safety, 
Tolerability, and Efficacy of AMG  145 on LDL-C in Subjects With Severe Familial 
Hypercholesterolemia 
 
[COMPANY_010] Protocol Number (AMG 145) [ADDRESS_145956] Number: 2011-005400-15 
Amendment Date: 02 December 2015 
 
Rationale:  
The protocol is being amended to: 
â€¢ Clarify end of study language to specify the study will end when the last patient 
has completed assessments at week 260. 
â€¢ Draw attention to collection of adverse device effects (ADEs) by [CONTACT_129353] (AEs) and serious adverse events (SAEs).  This information is 
already being collected under AEs. 
â€¢ Update criteria for possible drug-induced liver injury (DILI) . 
â€¢ Clarify language regarding product complaints. 
â€¢ Allow for additional pregnancy testing at the discretion of the investigator. 
â€¢ Correct Tanner Staging criteria for males.  
â€¢ Update pregnancy and lactation reporting language and added new sample 
reporting forms . 
â€¢ Correct typographic, grammatical, and formatting errors throughout the protocol .

Rationale:  
This document provides the rationale and detailed list of changes for Amendment 5, 
dated 11 May  2015, from Amendment 4 of the study protocol, dated 15 April 2014.  
The purpose of this amendment is:  
1. To remove the external Data Monitoring Committee (DMC) following the DMCâ€™s 
expressed preference to not review open- label, uncontrolled safety data. Safety 
monitoring will continue to be performed by [CONTACT_129355]. Even though review of this 
specific study will no longer fall under direct DMC review, the DMC will continue 
to consider the totality of data from all studies.  Any emerging safety 
considerations identified by [CONTACT_129356].   Additional minor editorial and typographical changes were also made. 
2. To add measurements of height, weight and Tanner staging for adolescent subjects, and to allow for documentation of historical assessments of height, weight and Tanner staging in adolescent subjects.   A definition of â€˜adolescentâ€™ 
was also provided.
